 How is the 20 rupee vial affluent to the farmers
 
 
 iskaa jeeta jaagta udhaaharan pankaj verma hai
 He quit his job as a private company of one and a half million and became a farmer and today with the help of this twenty rupee bottle of West decomposer, the French embassy is feeding the organic mushroom and the Australian embassy, kinnu
 yahaan nahin jis paraali jalaane kii samasya se pareshaan sarkaar ne sabsidi par paanch sau karod kharch kar die hon lekin bees rupye kii ek shishi kisaanon ke kahin zyaada kaam aa rahi he
 It is also finding a solution to the problem of straw and pesticides
 mana ja rahaa he ki ye shishi kheti kii laagat bahut kam kar sakati he or unhe munaafaa dilaa sakati he
 Pankaj Verma, a farmer living in Ghaziabad, says that the stubble is gold for him, this decomposer is nectar
 jabase unhone iskaa istemaal karnaa shuru kiya he khet kii sehat bad gai he
 There is no disease in the crop
 haryana ke kisaan amit kehete hai ki haryana ke saikadon kisaanon ko paraali jalaane se roka he
 Through this decomposer, the straw is converted into manure
 darasal yah koi jaadu nahin, shuddh vigyaan he
 This vial has a waste decomposer prepared from bacteria of cow dung and leaves
 jo mitti main jaivik parivartan or kechuen paidaa karte hai
 Through this, farmers like Pankaj Verma are earning millions of rupees by doing organic farming
 dikampoger kaa ye salution le jaakar 200 litre pani main do kilo gud gholkar dikampoger mila de
 After four days, spray the solution in the fields
 phir isi se das litre ghol nikaalkar 1000 litre dobaaraa ghol taiyaar kar sakate hai
 That is, once the solution is ready, farmers will not have to buy again and again
 punjab ke kinnu ke kisaan jitendra maavi bataate hai ki kinnu kii kheti par har saal wo saat lakh kaa pastiside prayog karte the aaj keval pachaas hajaar ke dikampoger se kinnu kii fasal ugaate hai
 This decomposer has been prepared by the National Organic Farming Center
 centre ke diarector kishan chandra bataate hai ki pichley saal se hi ye west compoger kisaanon ko diya ja rahe hai
 The most important thing about this waste decomposer is that the farmers can replicate it in their field and they do not need to use any insecticide after using it
 dilli sarkaar kii ore se prastaavit ek masauda paraamarsh main kaha gaya he ki rajya ke nijee aspataal aise marijon ke shav unke parijan ko saunpane se inkaar nahin kar sakate, jinaki maut ilaaj ke dauraan aspataal main hui ho or unke parivaaravale antyeshti se pehle bill kaa bhugtan karne main asamarth hon
 Delhi Health Minister Satyendar Jain said that this proposal does not mean that the bill was waived
 aspataal un pariwaron ke khilaaf kanoonee karrwai kar sakate hai jo baad main bhi bill kaa bhugtan nahin karenge
 There is also a proposal to reduce the bill in such cases, who die within 24 hours of hospitalization
 unhone kaha,“ agar koi marij aspataal ke immergency kaksh yaa cajmulti vibhaag main bhartee hone ke chah ghante ke bheetar dam tod detaa he to aspataal ko kul bill kaa 50 pratishat or 24 ghanton ke bheetar hone vaali maut ke maamle main 20 pratishat bill maaf kar dena chahie”
 He told a press conference, "no hospital can refuse to hand over the dead body of a patient to his family because of non-payment of bill
 maut ke baad shav samaaj kaa hota he or uski antyeshti jarur honi chahie”

 After the Telugu Desam Party came into existence, there was a big change in the politics of Andhra and the people of the state got an alternative in the form of TDP as another big party besides the Congress
 isi ke saath shrikakulam loksabhaa seat par bhi congress kaa prabhaav kaaphi teji se kam hua

 Politics of Srikakulam - TDP ended Congress 'raj' Politics in Srikakulam Lok Sabha seat has been very interesting
 is seat par 1952 main hue pehle aam chunaavon main rajagopala raav ne nirdaleey ummidavaar ke rup main jeet darj kii thi
 He defeated his rival IND candidate by a margin of 16 thousand votes
 haalanki loksabhaa chunaav jeetne ke baad unhone congress kaa daaman tham liya
 Rajgopala Rao, who started politics at the panchayat level, won the elections from Srikakulam Lok Sabha seat 6 times and reached Parliament
 is seat se sabase zyada baar loksabhaa chunaav jeetne kaa record bhi unheen ke naam darj he
 He won the general elections of 1952, 1957, 1962, 1971, 1977 and 1980
 haalanki, 1967 or 1967-71 ke aam chunaav main unhen kramash: swatantra party ke ummidavaar ji ranga or ji latachanna ke haathon haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 But then in the 1971 general election he defeated G
 Ranga by a huge margin of 1 lakh 37 thousand votes
 1982 main tidipi ke gathan ke baad hue aam chunaav (1984 main) main yah seat tidipi ke khate main chali gai
 But in Srikakulam, a stronghold of the Congress, returned again in the 1989 general elections and Congress candidate Vishwanath Kanithi defeated the then TDP MP by a margin of over 50,000 votes
 kanithi ne lagaataar do aam chunaav (1989-91, 1991-96) jite
 After 1996, the TDP made a tremendous comeback to the Srikakulam Lok Sabha under Yeron
 yeran naidu ne is seat par lagaataar chaar aam chunaav jite
 He won 1996, 98, 99 and 2004 four general elections
 dilachasp yah he ki is dauraan unka jeet kaa antar lagaataar badhata hi rahaa
